The current schema version is **42**, which is marked as final for the v1 dashboard API.\\n\\n### Frontend TypeScript Migration Layer\\n\\nThe frontend migration is implemented in `public/app/features/dashboard/state/DashboardMigrator.ts`, which defines `DASHBOARD_SCHEMA_VERSION = 42` and the `DashboardMigrator` class. This class implements the `updateSchema()` method that handles schema version migrations (v0-v42) directly in the browser. The related models are in:\\n\\n- `DashboardModel.ts` - Main dashboard data model with constructor defaults\\n- `PanelModel.ts` - Panel model with panel-specific defaults and migrations\\n- `TimeModel.ts` - Time range model\\n\\n### Backend Go Migration System\\n\\nThe backend migration system is located in `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/` and handles dashboard schema version migrations at runtime:\\n\\n#### Core Migration Orchestrator\\n- `migrate.go` - Main migration entry point with `Migrate()` function and `Initialize()` for dependency setup. Coordinates the migration pipeline including frontend defaults, schema version migrations, and cleanup.\\n- `frontend_defaults.go` - Applies DashboardModel and PanelModel constructor defaults to match frontend behavior\\n- `metrics.go` - Provides observability through metrics tracking\\n\\n#### Schema Version Migrations\\n- `schemaversion/migrations.go` - Core registry that defines `GetMigrations()` which maps schema versions (v2-v42) to their respective migration functions. Defines `SchemaVersionMigrationFunc` type and constants `LATEST_VERSION = 42` and `MIN_VERSION = 0`.\\n- `schemaversion/errors.go` - Error types including `MigrationError` and `MinimumVersionError`\\n- `schemaversion/v2.go` through `schemaversion/v42.go` - Individual migration functions (V2-V42) for each schema version. For example:\\n  - `V2` - Migrates legacy `services.filter` structure to modern `time` and `templating`\\n  - `V33` - Migrates datasource references from string names to structured UIDs using `DataSourceIndexProvider`\\n  - `V42` - Ensures fields hidden from visualization are also hidden from tooltips\\n\\n#### Migration Utilities\\n- `schemaversion/migration_utils.go` - Helper functions like `GetStringValue()`, `GetBoolValue()`, `GetIntValue()`, `GetFloatValue()` for safe type conversions\\n- `schemaversion/cache.go` - TTL-based caching mechanism with `cachedProvider` type for indexing datasources and library elements\\n- `schemaversion/datasource_utils.go` - `DatasourceIndex` for O(1) datasource lookups, `WrapIndexProviderWithCache()` for caching provider results\\n\\n### Conversion Layer\\n\\nThe conversion layer in `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/conversion/` handles transformations between different API versions:\\n\\n- `conversion.go` - Defines `DashboardConversion` interface and `RegisterConversions()` function that registers converters between API versions\\n- `v0.go`, `v1.go`, `v2.go` - Version-specific conversion implementations\\n- `v0alpha1_to_v1beta1.go` - Converts v0alpha1 dashboards to v1beta1\\n- `v1beta1_to_v2alpha1.go` - Converts v1beta1 dashboards to v2alpha1\\n- `v2alpha1_to_v1beta1.go` - Reverse conversion from v2alpha1 to v1beta1\\n- `v2alpha1_to_v2beta1.go` - Converts v2alpha1 to v2beta1\\n- `v2beta1_to_v2alpha1.go` - Reverse conversion from v2beta1 to v2alpha1\\n- `conversion_data_loss_detection.go` - Detects and tracks data loss during conversions\\n- `errors.go` and `metrics.go` - Error handling and observability for conversions\\n\\n### Legacy SQL Migration\\n\\nThe legacy SQL storage migration is implemented in `pkg/registry/apis/dashboard/legacy/`:\\n\\n- `sql_dashboards.go` - Implements `MigrateDashboards()` method that reads dashboards from legacy SQL storage and streams them to unified storage\\n- `types.go` - Defines `Migrator` interface with methods `MigrateDashboards()`, `MigrateFolders()`, `MigrateLibraryPanels()`\\n- `storage.go`, `client.go`, `context.go`, `queries.go`, `token.go` - Supporting infrastructure for legacy storage access\\n\\n### Migration Coordination\\n\\n- `pkg/registry/apis/dashboard/migrator/migrator.go` - Implements `FoldersDashboardsMigrator` interface via `foldersDashboardsMigrator` struct and `ProvideFoldersDashboardsMigrator()` function\\n- `pkg/registry/apis/dashboard/migration_registrar.go` - Registers the dashboard migration with the unified migration registry\\n\\n### Schema Definition and Validation\\n\\n- `pkg/kinds/dashboard/addenda.go` - Defines `HandoffSchemaVersion = 36` as the minimum schema version for Thema-based validation\\n- `apps/dashboard/pkg/apis/dashboard/v0alpha1/validation.go` and `v1beta1/validation.go` - Schema validation using `ValidateDashboardSpec()`\\n- `apps/dashboard/pkg/apis/dashboard/v0alpha1/conversion.go`, `v1beta1/conversion.go`, `v2alpha1/conversion.go`, `v2beta1/conversion.go` - Generated and manual conversion implementations\\n\\n### Key Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Dual-Path Migration**: Dashboards can be migrated either on the frontend (older versions) or backend (newer versions), with careful coordination to avoid double migration.\\n\\n2. **Field-Level Migrations**: Individual migration functions handle specific schema version changes, from simple property moves (v2) to complex datasource reference transformations (v33) to field configuration updates (v42).\\n\\n3. **Frontend Defaults Application**: The backend explicitly applies frontend DashboardModel and PanelModel constructor defaults to ensure consistency between frontend and backend processing.\\n\\n4. **Datasource Index Caching**: Migrations that reference datasources use a cached indexing system for efficient O(1) lookups.\\n\\n5. **Conversion Status Tracking**: The conversion layer tracks conversion metadata including source/target versions and any errors that occurred.\\n\\n6. **Version Pinning**: Schema version 42 is explicitly marked as final, with future panel-specific migrations to be implemented in individual panel plugin migration handlers rather than as new dashboard schema versions.\\n\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2769,"cache_read_input_tokens":82501,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2769},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"fc4fb9b3-e817-4186-8b9a-d6cc1991078d","uuid":"df53c637-d4f3-4f86-b5fa-0a03abb46f8f"}

comprehensive dashboard JSON schema versioning and migration system across both frontend (TypeScript) and backend (Go) layers. The current schema version is **42**, which is marked as final for the v1 dashboard API.\\n\\n### Frontend TypeScript Migration Layer\\n\\nThe frontend migration is implemented in `public/app/features/dashboard/state/DashboardMigrator.ts`, which defines `DASHBOARD_SCHEMA_VERSION = 42` and the `DashboardMigrator` class. This class implements the `updateSchema()` method that handles schema version migrations (v0-v42) directly in the browser. The related models are in:\\n\\n- `DashboardModel.ts` - Main dashboard data model with constructor defaults\\n- `PanelModel.ts` - Panel model with panel-specific defaults and migrations\\n- `TimeModel.ts` - Time range model\\n\\n### Backend Go Migration System\\n\\nThe backend migration system is located in `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/` and handles dashboard schema version migrations at runtime:\\n\\n#### Core Migration Orchestrator\\n- `migrate.go` - Main migration entry point with `Migrate()` function and `Initialize()` for dependency setup. Coordinates the migration pipeline including frontend defaults, schema version migrations, and cleanup.\\n- `frontend_defaults.go` - Applies DashboardModel and PanelModel constructor defaults to match frontend behavior\\n- `metrics.go` - Provides observability through metrics tracking\\n\\n#### Schema Version Migrations\\n- `schemaversion/migrations.go` - Core registry that defines `GetMigrations()` which maps schema versions (v2-v42) to their respective migration functions. Defines `SchemaVersionMigrationFunc` type and constants `LATEST_VERSION = 42` and `MIN_VERSION = 0`.\\n- `schemaversion/errors.go` - Error types including `MigrationError` and `MinimumVersionError`\\n- `schemaversion/v2.go` through `schemaversion/v42.go` - Individual migration functions (V2-V42) for each schema version. For example:\\n  - `V2` - Migrates legacy `services.filter` structure to modern `time` and `templating`\\n  - `V33` - Migrates datasource references from string names to structured UIDs using `DataSourceIndexProvider`\\n  - `V42` - Ensures fields hidden from visualization are also hidden from tooltips\\n\\n#### Migration Utilities\\n- `schemaversion/migration_utils.go` - Helper functions like `GetStringValue()`, `GetBoolValue()`, `GetIntValue()`, `GetFloatValue()` for safe type conversions\\n- `schemaversion/cache.go` - TTL-based caching mechanism with `cachedProvider` type for indexing datasources and library elements\\n- `schemaversion/datasource_utils.go` - `DatasourceIndex` for O(1) datasource lookups, `WrapIndexProviderWithCache()` for caching provider results\\n\\n### Conversion Layer\\n\\nThe conversion layer in `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/conversion/` handles transformations between different API versions:\\n\\n- `conversion.go` - Defines `DashboardConversion` interface and `RegisterConversions()` function that registers converters between API versions\\n- `v0.go`, `v1.go`, `v2.go` - Version-specific conversion implementations\\n- `v0alpha1_to_v1beta1.go` - Converts v0alpha1 dashboards to v1beta1\\n- `v1beta1_to_v2alpha1.go` - Converts v1beta1 dashboards to v2alpha1\\n- `v2alpha1_to_v1beta1.go` - Reverse conversion from v2alpha1 to v1beta1\\n- `v2alpha1_to_v2beta1.go` - Converts v2alpha1 to v2beta1\\n- `v2beta1_to_v2alpha1.go` - Reverse conversion from v2beta1 to v2alpha1\\n- `conversion_data_loss_detection.go` - Detects and tracks data loss during conversions\\n- `errors.go` and `metrics.go` - Error handling and observability for conversions\\n\\n### Legacy SQL Migration\\n\\nThe legacy SQL storage migration is implemented in `pkg/registry/apis/dashboard/legacy/`:\\n\\n- `sql_dashboards.go` - Implements `MigrateDashboards()` method that reads dashboards from legacy SQL storage and streams them to unified storage\\n- `types.go` - Defines `Migrator` interface with methods `MigrateDashboards()`, `MigrateFolders()`, `MigrateLibraryPanels()`\\n- `storage.go`, `client.go`, `context.go`, `queries.go`, `token.go` - Supporting infrastructure for legacy storage access\\n\\n### Migration Coordination\\n\\n- `pkg/registry/apis/dashboard/migrator/migrator.go` - Implements `FoldersDashboardsMigrator` interface via `foldersDashboardsMigrator` struct and `ProvideFoldersDashboardsMigrator()` function\\n- `pkg/registry/apis/dashboard/migration_registrar.go` - Registers the dashboard migration with the unified migration registry\\n\\n### Schema Definition and Validation\\n\\n- `pkg/kinds/dashboard/addenda.go` - Defines `HandoffSchemaVersion = 36` as the minimum schema version for Thema-based validation\\n- `apps/dashboard/pkg/apis/dashboard/v0alpha1/validation.go` and `v1beta1/validation.go` - Schema validation using `ValidateDashboardSpec()`\\n- `apps/dashboard/pkg/apis/dashboard/v0alpha1/conversion.go`, `v1beta1/conversion.go`, `v2alpha1/conversion.go`, `v2beta1/conversion.go` - Generated and manual conversion implementations\\n\\n### Key Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Dual-Path Migration**: Dashboards can be migrated either on the frontend (older versions) or backend (newer versions), with careful coordination to avoid double migration.\\n\\n2. **Field-Level Migrations**: Individual migration functions handle specific schema version changes, from simple property moves (v2) to complex datasource reference transformations (v33) to field configuration updates (v42).\\n\\n3. **Frontend Defaults Application**: The backend explicitly applies frontend DashboardModel and PanelModel constructor defaults to ensure consistency between frontend and backend processing.\\n\\n4. **Datasource Index Caching**: Migrations that reference datasources use a cached indexing system for efficient O(1) lookups.\\n\\n5. **Conversion Status Tracking**: The conversion layer tracks conversion metadata including source/target versions and any errors that occurred.\\n\\n6. **Version Pinning**: Schema version 42 is explicitly marked as final, with future panel-specific migrations to be implemented in individual panel plugin migration handlers rather than as new dashboard schema versions.\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
